TEXT: 
Click start and then click control panel or point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click administrative tools.
Double-Click services.
Double-Click messenger.
In the startup type list click disabled.
Click stop and then click ok.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), click(control,panel), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(administrative,tools), double-click(services), double-click(messenger), click(disabled), click(stop), click(ok)

TEXT: 
On the tools menu click folder options.
On the view tab click to clear the hide protected operating system files check box.

ACTIONS: 
click(folder,options), click(box), clear(check,box)

click(folder,options), click(box), clear(check,box)TEXT: 
Click start point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click system.
On the hardware tab click device manager.
In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.
On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(system), click(device,manager), click(plus,symbol), click(cdrw/dvd,drive), click(properties), click(prompted), select(prompted), click(ok), restart(computer)

TEXT: 
Click start point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click system.
On the hardware tab click device manager.
In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.
On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

ACTIONS:

Click start point to settings and then click control panel.

On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

On the hardware tab click device manager.
In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.
On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(system), click(device,manager), click(plus,symbol), click(cdrw/dvd,drive), click(properties), click(prompted), select(prompted), click(ok), restart(computer)

TEXT: 
Click start and then click control panel or point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click administrative tools.
Double-Click services.
Double-Click messenger.
In the startup type list click disabled.
Click stop and then click ok.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), click(control,panel), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(administrative,tools), double-click(services), double-click(messenger), click(disabled), click(stop), click(ok)

TEXT: 
On the tools menu click folder options.
On the view tab click to clear the hide protected operating system files check box.

ACTIONS: 
click(folder,options), click(box), clear(check,box)

On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

Click start point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click system.
On the hardware tab click device manager.
In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.
On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

TEXT: 
Click start point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click system.

On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

On the hardware tab click device manager.
In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.
On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(system), click(device,manager), click(plus,symbol), click(cdrw/dvd,drive), click(properties), click(prompted), select(prompted), click(ok), restart(computer)

TEXT: 
Click start and then click control panel or point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click administrative tools.
Double-Click services.
Double-Click messenger.
In the startup type list click disabled.
Click stop and then click ok.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), click(control,panel), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(administrative,tools), double-click(services), double-click(messenger), click(disabled), click(stop), click(ok)

TEXT: 
On the tools menu click folder options.
On the view tab click to clear the hide protected operating system files check box.

ACTIONS: 
click(folder,options), click(box), clear(check,box)

click(folder,options), click(box), clear(check,box)

TEXT: 
Click start point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click system.
On the hardware tab click device manager.
In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.
On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(system), click(device,manager), click(plus,symbol), click(cdrw/dvd,drive), click(properties), click(prompted), select(prompted), click(ok), restart(computer)

On the action menu click properties.
On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.
Click ok and then restart your computer when you are prompted.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(system), click(device,manager), click(plus,symbol), click(cdrw/dvd,drive), click(properties), click(prompted), select(prompted), click(ok), restart(computer)

TEXT: 
Click start point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click system.

In device manager click the plus symbol next to dvd/cd-rom drives and then click your cdrw/dvd drive.

On the properties tab click to select the enable digital cd audio for this cd-rom device.

TEXT: 
Click start and then click control panel or point to settings and then click control panel.
Double-Click administrative tools.
Double-Click services.
Double-Click messenger.
In the startup type list click disabled.
Click stop and then click ok.

ACTIONS: 
click(start), click(control,panel), point(settings), click(control,panel), double-click(administrative,tools), double-click(services), double-click(messenger), click(disabled), click(stop), click(ok)

TEXT: 
On the tools menu click folder options.
On the view tab click to clear the hide protected operating system files check box.

ACTIONS: 
click(folder,options), click(box), clear(check,box)
